< review>
This place is genuine, Rick and the staff have years of experience and gray staff that pay attention to detail.
They explain everything in a way anyone can understand. No games, real fair pricing, very timely and great warranty on what they fix. Usually during the holidays mechanics can best you up on price but not here.
It never felt awkward, never pressured, just welcomed.
They show you the parts they fix and they follow call you up a couple days after to ensure quality/answers. Lastly, they sanitize the vehicle before and after. This is my new family. Thanks Dorso's and happy Holidays.<//review>

Shawn Pitman< /username>
<time>1616430921395< /time>< Rate>
5<//Rate>
< Text>
I dealt with Joe and Rick (hope I got your name right!).

Firstly, this was my first experience getting maintenance done in the bay area. So I was ready for some sticker shock. I had rear pads and rotors + oil change.

I was advised very well about what needed to be done, and what was recommended. I requested a few extra services be skipped and Dorso's obliged without complaint. So the sales approach is low pressure and friendly.

My only complaint was that I wasn't offered anything other than OEM or preferred parts. "Back home" many shops will offer cheaper (new) parts with your approval and if you waive a warranty on the service. I was NOT offered this and as a result the total was very pricey.

Lastly, I was entirely pleased with the professionalism. All removed parts were kept and shown to me. Everyone was very friendly. No one got upset when I refused additional services. And future service recommendations (and where to get them) were provided.

Dorso's seems like a great first stop for your auto service. In the future I might comparison price shop a bit before plunking down a ton of money for something I used to be able to do in my own driveway for 1/10th the cost. But perhaps that's just the way things are in the Bay Area... And since I can't service my own cars anymore, maybe I need to adjust my expectations.<//Text>

< Review>
I went to smaller garages to have my 2003 Tacoma fixed for failing smog due to a fuel EVAP system-related check engine code.

I paid a lot to have a thorough diagnostic performed, and the quote to replace my fuel EVAP canister (aka charcoal canister) was even more than I had already spent at other garages, so it was a little discouraging at first.

However, in addition to this quote I got the full technical report which was highly professional. They were also willing to answer my questions that came up as I tried to replace the canister myself.

Ultimately I was able to do the replacement myself and clear the code to successfully pass smog. The relatively expensive diagnostic was money well spent at Dorso‚Äôs, because I was able to take the report and figure out exactly what to do and ended up saving money. They are very competent and provided excellent support. I will absolutely return to them in the future whenever my family‚Äôs vehicles have complex problems.< /Review>

< review>
After having two vehicles to this shop recently, one of which involving a non-typical engine mechanical problem, I am extremely pleased with the results.  The mechanics and leadership are professional, highly competent, and respectful in their relationships with customers.  Though not a normal repair for them, I was impressed with their diagnostic knowledge and capability, and effectiveness in researching potential issues with my '03 Z06 Corvette.  They handled the replacement of a broken valve spring, and the other 15 springs per my request, along with some other work in outstanding fashion.  They may not be the cheapest, but when you consider the technology, special tooling, and staffing requirements to handle these types of repairs well, they are a true value in comparison with a dealership and other less capable shops.  I was also impressed by the level of transparency and honesty, and loved their attention to gathering and tracking all historical data associated with the car for current and future reference. < Review>
I love this gym! It is the cleanest gym that I have ever worked out at and the staff are amazing. I've previously lived in LA, where I frequently worked out at Crunch Gym, LA fitness, and a couple other small joints around my area. Although this gym is small, there is never that many people in there that would ruin your workout. I workout 6 days a week and always can find a spot to lift and jump rope in-between sets. I really appreciate how they provide towels for sweat and a many bottles of disinfectant to clean the equipment with. At Crunch Fitness, they started charging you monthly just to have a small towel. Cleanliness of a gym I believe is extremely important. I once got a flesh eating bacteria on my hands and neck from other gyms. It cost quite a pretty penny for a poor college student to deal with. I recommend this gym to everyone I meet who is looking for a great place to workout.</Review>

<Review>If you're reading this to decide whether or not you want to move to Atlas, I'll tell you right now the answer is unequivocally, yes. My husband and I have lived here for a little over one year now (moved from San Francisco to Atlas in Oakland at the end of May 2020) and are blown away by several key factors here: the staff, apartment design features (interiors and exteriors), amenity spaces and the apartment events.

The staff:

Joseph was the first person we met at Atlas and helped us throughout the entire leasing process last year. His energy was super contagious and even though some features of Atlas were not yet complete/opened at that time (due to the building being in new construction AND the pandemic) he was able to bring us completely on board with his excitement in the upcoming (but now open) spaces and features. Other members of the leasing staff (Addison, India, Alfonso) and management, (Amy and Selwyn), are the best team I've ever encountered. Our maintenance staff as well is incredibly responsive, friendly and a key role in keeping everything here so beautiful.

Concierge staff is 24/7 and once you move in you'll be quick to recognize these friendly faces: Roosevelt, Richard, Brayan and more! Not only are they all incredibly helpful in answering questions involving the in's-and-out's of the building and its features, but this team is so ridiculously kind and patient and somehow know every. single. resident. here (and there are a lot of us...). They are some of the first faces you'll get to know and likely will be the individuals you talk to everyday (whether that's just to chat or ask questions).

Apartment design + amenity spaces:
Every single color, light fixture, piece of furniture, and even down to their insanely popular coffee machine, is intentional. My friends tell me they feel like they're at a 5 star hotel or luxury resort.

Their gym? Chef's kiss. Cancel your Equinox membership.

The 41st floor has a huge game room, separate movie theatre lounge and an absolutely stunning cocktail and private dining lounge. I don't want to spoil the surprise but fairly certain your jaw will drop once you see it. The 4th floor also has amenities like a co-working (WeWork-like) space, pool, hot tub, grill and event space. There is also the 3rd floor (outdoor) pet park that undergoes extensive cleanings multiple times a day, and is next to their pet wash room.

Apartment events:
The events here are so, so fun (and there are a ton to choose from). Not only are these a great way to meet your neighbors (everyone is incredibly social here), but it's also a wonderful way to learn about local businesses in the area. There's a mix of food / cocktail events either in the amenity spaces (where the spread is, again, chef's kiss) or hosted at the actual restaurants / bars themselves! Supporting the local community is so important to me, and I'm sure many others, and Atlas has done an incredible job in making sure we get to know the community we live in. In addition to food events, we've had things like dessert and wine tasting events, pub crawls, monthly first Friday events hosted by a neighboring bar called The Golden Bull (which is apparently owned by one of the members of Green Day!), 2x weekly Swyft HIIT classes and 1x weekly Swyft Yoga classes, painting and cooking classes and more.

I will also mention just how unmatched the level of security here is.  24/7 building security patrolling the perimeters and inside the building. Your packages are secured in a lockage storage system and the parking garage is equally as secure and patrolled by building security. I haven't had any issues with our car here - I accidentally left my wallet in my car overnight and my car was totally fine (and the wallet was still there!).

If you couldn't tell, my husband and I love Atlas. I could go on and on about this place and how amazing it is, but you'll just have to see it to get what I'm saying. If you're still debating - just look at the other 100+ 5 star reviews on this place and see how it speaks for itself.</Review>< Pics>

<UserId.>112009386938690483282< /UserId.><time>1609969818121</time>< Text>
TLDR: You won't regret moving to this beautiful community. It's not too good to be true, it's literally just the perfect place to live.

Atlas is SUCH wonderful place to live. I had the pleasure of working with Addison, who was incredible during the whole process of finding the right unit. Because of COVID and this being my first apartment, I had a TON of questions and took some time to tour (which he graciously let me do more than once because I was indecisive) and eventually signed the lease. He was SO patient and helpful the whole time, answering any questions I had, and I was eventually comfortable enough to make the decision to move here. Even when I signed the lease and had more questions about next steps, he was always ready to help and I really appreciated that.

When I moved in about a month ago, I was given my keys and upon entering my unit was greeted by a really lovely welcome gift. The quality of the units are fantastic: the floors, cabinets, appliances. Everything!

I had a bit of an ant problem when I moved in, not a trail but more like a few here and there (common with new construction) but the maintenance team was incredibly quick to add some caulking in the bathroom for me and schedule pest control! I haven't had any problems since.

What's really nice too, though I haven't used them yet, is the amenities. You definitely get what you pay for in a community like this. The concierge service, the work rooms, community events (COVID friendly), the gym space that we will soon have, etc.

Other random things I love:
- The windows, especially great when it's raining
- The bathroom tub is the most luxurious thing I've ever seen lol
- Front load washer and dryer
- Deep kitchen sink + pullout sprayer
- The heater gets really hot
- Staff is literally always friendly (I.E there have been times that I'm carrying a million groceries and one of the concierge will open the door for me and press my floor in the elevator which I think is really kind) + it doesn't end once you've signed the lease like other places that get your money and kind of drop the ball
- There's an app for the building where you can pay your rent, RSVP for events, check out local events in the area, etc

If you're thinking about this place, go for it! I can honestly say that I made a great decision moving here.< /Text>

< text>
I've been purposely holding off on reviewing, wanted to give a fair assessment now nearly 6 months into our time at Atlas. We were among the first to occupy the tower, have seen steady progress wrt both completion/availability of amenities and resident move-ins.

Property: We've experienced minor hiccups as are to be expected with new construction: sewage odor leak from toilet, defective window, for example. All issues have been rectified. The building really is beautiful. And views from the 41st- floor community spaces: unmatched.

Staff: You'll interact on the daily with the concierge desk; these folks are some of the greatest people you'll ever meet. Super helpful and patient. Office and maintenance staff are great, too. With so much movement on the property, you'd expect requests would either go ignored or untouched for weeks. Responses are timely, service completed with a smile.

Neighbors: We're not yet sharing walls with anyone, so can't comment on noise, though will point out that sound carries up from the pool, so keep that in mind when selecting unit location.

Overall: We feel as though we live on a resort. Yes, rates are high. Though you get what you pay for: community events like yoga and HIIT classes, many free meals + booze, a well-designed gym with top-of-line equipment, package delivery management and so much more!<//text>

< text>
I recently toured the Atlas Apartments in Oakland, in search of my new home. Pretty early into viewing the amenities throughout the building, it was clear that of all the apartment communities I had seen thus far, Atlas was exceptional. You can see the thought that went into the design and spaces for gathering, working, entertaining and relaxing. The apartments are very well-appointed with solid and quality finishes, and that includes solid real wood doors (a personal highlight for me). If you are lucky to take a tour with Joseph, the leasing manager, you'll be in excellent hands. < Review>
I moved into Atlas in August and, having moved between many apartments across a couple of continents, I can truly say that this is the best apartment building I have ever lived in. The building itself is beautifully finished and boasts amazing views out over Oakland. It is also situated very close to the lake and many bars and restaurants. While the amenities in the building are largely closed due to the ongoing pandemic, the team at Atlas has made every effort to bring joy to the community by offering fitness classes and a variety of virtual events, my favourite of which is the virtual happy hour on the first Friday of each month where cocktails from the golden bull are brought directly do the doors of residents' apartments, free of charge.

Though the apartments and the amenities are outstanding in themselves, the aspect of Atlas that sets it apart from other apartment buildings is its team. Roosevelt and Richard are both so friendly, and personable, and incredibly helpful; it's always a pleasure to see them in the foyer. When I toured the building before moving in, I was shown around by Joseph who was more than happy to answer any questions and did not exert any pressure to rush into any decisions, which was very refreshing. On the day that I moved there were a few hiccoughs (read: Uhaul last-minute cancellation) and Joseph went to great lengths to help make things run as smoothly as possible. He is an asset to Atlas, and in the months following my move, he has been consistently affable and accommodating; a genuine delight to interact with. Whatever the situation, the team go above and beyond, be it taking deliveries, calling the lift for you when your hands are full, or even just having some friendly chit chat. I would thoroughly recommend Atlas to anyone who is looking for a luxury apartment community within Oakland.<//Review>

< text>
Initially I was quite pleased with NRG, but as the project progressed, it appeared as though there was a significant disconnect within the company's communication pathways. There were unnecessary delays caused by the NRG using old and outdated forms that were submitted to Edison for compliance and inspection. This required me to be present not once, but twice, which cut into my work schedule. Between project design delays and installation delays and the inspection delays, it put the job 2 months behind the target date. I made several calls into NRG but never got the problems handled in a timely manner, hence the 2 month delay in getting solar hooked up and running!
Since then, we had a very wet winter and I had a roof leak, not knowing if it was due to NRG's work or not. I called my own roofer, who on inspection, found left over parts and supplies from NRG that were left on the roof, causing water to dam and pool. He removed the parts to allow the water to flow. I called NRG to notify them and asked them if they would repair the interior dry wall damage, resulting from their crew leaving items on the roof. They declined, saying that there's no proof that it was due to their negligence, as my roofer removed the items causing the initial water pooling. They demanded pictures from the roofer to prove that items were left on the roof, and a signed letter from him, stating that he removed the items, and to provide his contractor license number. They further stated that most people lack honesty and that they have to protect themselves from such customers.

I have been a homeowner for 34 years, having completed 2 major remodels, and am a CPA formerly auditing both small and large businesses. I have never experienced a business questioning my veracity, nor a company that would not at the very least send out a tech to inspect the leak. The damages were $200. The install was $26,000. No matter what I said to the manager, I was rebuked. I then decided to post this review.

Since then, I received a call from the Operations Manager stating that it is company policy not to service customers who have posted a negative review, but assured me the repair would be done if I pulled the review.

No matter how happy I am that I went solar, I am highly disappointed in a company that lacks integrity to this degree. In my opinion, it's a poor choice not to remedy such a small repair for such a large installation. It's also not in their best interest to doubt customers without reason, nor to try to bribe them to remove a review.
Customers don't always remember the product, but they will always remember the service they received, or didn't.< /text>

<user>103748551017913986634< /user>< Text>
I visited here for a Saturday brunch. Nice European-style bakery.

PRO: I had Moon over Norway (ham, poached egg, cheese, etc) and the stuff inside the crepe was EXCELLENT. Poached eggs were so good and just the overall flavor was great. Nice patio. Chocolate macaroon (the coconut flake thing, not the colourful mini-burger looking thing) was good. Almont croissant was good... like 7.5~8 out of 10.

CON: The actual crepes. They were hard, rubbery, difficult to cut, and too chewy. I thought they were more like the Chinese scallion pancakes, but even tougher. Service felt a bit on the slow side.

I give it 3 stars plus 1 more star for the excellent crepe filling.<//Text>
